) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

-- Table structure for table `failed_jobs`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `failed_jobs`;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `failed_jobs` (
  `id` bigint UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `uuid` varchar(191) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `connection` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `queue` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `payload` longtext CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `exception` longtext CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `failed_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `failed_jobs_uuid_unique` (`uuid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Table structure for table `users`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `users`;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `users` (
  `user_create_id` int NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `user_create_date` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `user_idname` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `name` text,
  `user_password` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `user_verified_date` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `user_account_status` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `user_last_login` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `last_password_change` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `force_reset` int DEFAULT '0',
  `updated_at` datetime DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `created_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`user_create_id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=633 DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

--
-- Table structure for table `verifytoken`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `verifytoken`;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `verifytoken` (
  `verify_id` int NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `user_idname` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `verify_token` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `token_create` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00 00:00:00',
  `token_expiry` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00 00:00:00',
  PRIMARY KEY (`verify_id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=752 DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;
